The news are collected automatically from a huge amount of <a href=\"/novostnye-sayty-runeta___news\">news</a>, <a href=\"/sayty-o-kriptovalyutah-rus___news\">Russian</a> and <a href=\"/sayty-o-kriptovalyutah-eng___news\">English</a> specialized websites with 24/7 updates.<br><br> \n- regularly updated <a href=\"/kriptovaluta\">cryptocurrency </a> and <a href=\"/birzha\">cryptocurrency exchange website</a> directories. We monitor the emergence of new Bitcoin and  Litecoin forks in order to add them into our database. This allows traders and investors not to miss a new, profitable coin or platform.<br><br>\n- the section <a href=\"/mining\">Mining</a> profitability rating allows you to get the most of the computing power of your existing equipment and choose the most profitable cryptocurrency for mining. The section <a href=\"/pools\">mining pools</a>will help you choose a quality pool.<br><br> \n- <a href=\"/_kurs__grafik\">Exchange rate fluctuation</a> and <a href=\"/_objom__grafik\">Transaction volume fluctuation</a> charts for various cryptocurrencies will help you make the right decision in matters of buying and selling cryptocurrency. <a href=\"/_slozhnost__grafik\">Mining difficulty</a> and <a href=\"/_objom__grafik\">network capacity</a> charts will also be useful to the miner.<br><br> \nWe’ve tried to gather all the necessary tools for cryptocurrency market analysis in one place
